<rate>3</rate>< Review>
Call ahead by more than three hours so they can go get the tires you ordered from their depot in time for your appointment, otherwise it will get pushed back. Make sure to specify which tires are to be replaced. Ask for their free 78% nitrogen (fresh air) instead of 100% nitrogen to avoid a surprise $8 per tire later. Get ready for the call halfway through the 90 minute operation offering a raft of unnecessary repairs including replacing any other new tires you might have installed that you didnt ask to be replaced. They will remove any tire pressure monitoring (TPMS) stems you may have and replace them and charge you $8 each. When you get home be sure to deflate the tires from the 42 psi they overinflated them to. There is a brand new Harley Davidson parked out front you can admire while you queue. They use nice flat hydraulic lifts.< /Review>

I don't leave review often. However, I'm very happy with the service I received at American Tire Depot.

I recently hit a pot hole and blew out a tire.  After the tire replacement (which I did at another place), my vehicle started to pull to the right.

Do not take your pet to Dr. Moore's veterinary clinic.
Barnabus, our rabbit, was killed there yesterday. He was only 3 years old and perfectly healthy.
We took him in to Moore Veterinary Clinic here in Ventura for a check up and urinalysis. Due to very poor handling by Dr. Moore and her staff, they caused Barnabus to go into shock. He died within minutes in their care. The last thing I heard was a loud squeal from Barnabus. I was in complete shock. I didnt know what to say or how to react. I patted him on the head before they took him to the back for the urinalysis, then minutes later I was looking at his dead body. He had bonded mates that he does not get to return to and they dont get to understand his absence.

I cant recommend you avoid Moore Veterinary clinic enough. If you dont believe me, then at the very least NEVER let them take your pet out of your sight.

It was a betrayal. I was in shock and had no words. This is a senseless tragedy and we are still mourning and dumbfounded by it.

PLEASE DO NOT TAKE YOUR PET TO MOORE VETERINARY CLINIC. I fear for the safety of any animals that enter there. If a veterinarian and her staff cannot do a simple thing such as handle an animal safely, how can you possibly trust Dr. Moores judgment and diagnosis?<//Review>
< name>
Bradley Walters< /name>
< resp>
{'time': 1580588315784, 'text': 'I understand how upsetting the sudden loss of your rabbit, Barnabus, is to you. I am deeply saddened by this as well, and offer my condolences to you and your wife, Anastassia. Rabbits and other defined prey species are considered delicate animals as they have evolved a known reaction to fearful or stressful situations. Many veterinarians will not treat them because of this internal biological response, that can lead to an unforeseeable collapse and/or death. This flooding of flight or fight sympathetic autonomic nervous system hormones, like epinephrine, can lead to cardiac abnormalities or other acute failures. Rabbits do require calm, careful approaches to examining and treating them. Because Barnabus was somewhat stressed from the exam, I tried to let him calm down in his kennel for several minutes. Because of your observation of a dark (presumed) urine, a urinalysis was recommended and authorized. He was carefully bundled in a towel to hopefully keep calm, secure, and to protect from bucking. After the procedure, we attempted to rewrap him and return him. Unfortunately, he leapt out of the bundle, and while trying to catch him before harm could come to him, he seemed to suffer the prey syndrome. Despite our attempts to immediately treat him for this medical event, we were not successful. Please know there was not any inappropriate or negligent action. I am distressed this occurred and am sorry. These unpredictable events are heartbreaking for everyone involved. We try very hard to lower risk factors leading to this known, albeit horrifying, syndrome. Again, I am very sorry for your anguish and beyond saddened for your loss of your family member.'}< /resp>

< Review>
What it lacks in size, it makes up for in heart. Comics For The Win has it all: comics, trading cards, memorabilia, snacks, a bathroom with above-average amenities (and feminine hygiene products to boot!), and best of all, an owner who cares about his relationship with his customers. Kris Bartolome genuinely wants you to enjoy your visit to Comics FTW. He makes an effort to learn the name of everyone who walks in the door. He listens to the community and is always open to input. If you like comics, but hate stereotypical comic stores, Comics FTW is for you.<//Review>

<UserId.>108669218287268111690</UserId.><name>Nathaniel Maghanoy<//name><Date>1514679110642< /Date><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Remember that super chill dude you met at the first Comic/Gaming shop you visited who was friendly, accepted you for who you are, and was just as passionate about the stuff you were into? Yeah he runs this place.

I hadnt bought a comic since the early 90s. Now that Im technically an adult with disposable income, I wanted to find a local Comic/Gaming shop to re-ignite the imagination that mundane modern life tries to extinguish.

After my garbage(and only) experience at Outer Planes in Downtown Santa Rosa, Google directed me to Comics FTW and thank the gods it did. Outer Planes is unaware of the business pillar known as Customer Service.

This is a store for comic lovers, by a comic lover. Dont let the small space fool you, the walls are bursting with selections from your more mainstream Marvel and DC fare to Alt-Genres galore. As a massive horror, sci-fi, and fantasy lover, there was more than enough for me to pour over. My girlfriend has slightly less dark sensibilities than me and her interest was piqued every few feet.

In addition to literature they have some pretty rad figurines that ranged from the small Japanese Gachapon type, to action figures, to the larger foot tall models. ㄢThe owner was more than happy to order some series he didnt have on hand for me, even ordered me the newest D&D Players Handbook and Dungeon Masters Guide despite that not being a focus of theirs. Didnt expect to drop $300 bucks on comics, RPGs Core Books, and sushi shaped toys, but this little shop of wonders has me hooked and I will be back on the monthly.

Support a local business and visit this shop, unless you want Barnes and Noble or the tools at Outer Planes to be the last brick and mortar graphic novel shop in town.<//text>

< Review>
One of the best locations in this area. It is conveniently next to the 405 freeway and the parking is good since its connected to a very large lot of other businesses. Drive thru is usually busy. The food here is quite good and consistent from the years I have eaten here. Always get the in-house made Natural Lemonade with free refills (I have been avoiding corn syrup based fountain drinks).  Customer service actually seems nice and helpful (not scripted compared to some other fast food chains). Location is well kept as well. Definitely a good fast food place to eat at.< /Review>

One of my go to places when I'm hungry. Started going here when I was in college and fell in love with Wendy's. My favorite is still a frosty with a chili. Now this is added their beautiful dinner salads I have a lot more choices.
I usually drive through, so I can only tell you that the outside of the building is always kept extremely clean. The last time I was through their speaker system wasn't working so they had a very beautiful young lady taking our orders and sending them through her headset to be made and placed in bags.
One of the reasons I love to go to Wendy's is because of their work with adoptions and the adoption system. The gentleman who started Wendy's was an adopted baby. he's always felt that his upbringing is what made him able to go into the world and make a name for himself. The name of the business Wendy's was named after his daughter. It's a wonderful story.
The food pricing is very minimal. I have never had anything that wasn't delectable. And they always seem to have a friendly smile when I'm either in drive-up line or inside the building.
If you enjoyed my review, please LIKE me below and if you get a chance please RATE me. As always thank you for your time and energy. Have an amazing life!<//text>

At any rate it's an easy place to stop at if you happen to be heading north.<//review>
